--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View VWALLACCOUNT
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "AUCTION"."VWALLACCOUNT" ("SEQ", "EMAIL", "NAME", "PW", "ADDRESS", "BIRTH", "REGDATE", "TEL", "BONUS") AS 
  select m.seq as seq,m.email, name, pw, address, birth, regdate, tel, bonus from tblMember m inner join tblMemberDetail md
    on m.seq = md.seq
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View VWAUCTIONINFO
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "AUCTION"."VWAUCTIONINFO" ("SEQ", "SELLERSEQ", "TITLE", "GOODNAME", "DETAIL", "BRAND", "STARTPRICE", "REGTIME", "DEADLINE", "INSTANTPRICE", "ASKINGPRICE", "GOODSSIZE", "NOWPRICE", "SELLERNAME", "SELLEREMAIL", "BIGCATEGORY", "SMALLCATEGORY", "SMALLCATEGORYSEQ", "MAINIMG") AS 
  select a.seq as seq,m.seq as sellerseq, a.title as title, a.goodname as goodname,a.detail as detail,a.brand as brand, a.startprice,
a.regtime as regtime, a.deadline as deadline, a.instantprice as instantprice, a.askingprice as askingprice,
a.goodssize, a.nowprice, m.name as sellername, m.email as selleremail,gbc.category as bigcategory, gsc.category as smallcategory, gsc.seq as smallcategoryseq,
(select image from tblAuctionImage where auctionseq=a.seq and ismain = 1) as mainimg
from tblAuctionGoods a inner join tblMember m 
                                        on a.memberseq = m.seq inner join tblGoodsSmallCategory gsc
                                                on gsc.seq = a.smallcategoryseq inner join tblGoodsBigCategory gbc
                                                    on gbc.seq = gsc.bigcategoryseq
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View VWAXX
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "AUCTION"."VWAXX" ("GOODNAME", "STATUS", "BIDDINGPRICE", "FINALBIDDINGPRICE") AS 
  select "GOODNAME","STATUS","BIDDINGPRICE","FINALBIDDINGPRICE" from (select ag.goodname as goodname, ts.status as status, b.biddingprice as biddingprice, (select max(tblBid.biddingprice) from tblBid where tblBid.auctionseq = b.auctionseq) as finalbiddingprice from tblBid b inner join tblAuctiongoods ag on b.auctionseq = ag.seq inner join tblauctionstatus ts on b.auctionstatusseq = ts.seq where b.memberseq = 1) where biddingprice = (select max(biddingprice) from (select ag.goodname, ts.status, b.biddingprice, (select max(tblBid.biddingprice) from tblBid where tblBid.auctionseq = b.auctionseq) as finalbiddingprice from tblBid b inner join tblAuctiongoods ag on b.auctionseq = ag.seq inner join tblauctionstatus ts on b.auctionstatusseq = ts.seq ))
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View VWBIDHISTORY
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "AUCTION"."VWBIDHISTORY" ("IMAGENAME", "SEQ", "TITLE", "STATUS", "BIDDINGPRICE", "BIGPRICE", "MEMBERSEQ") AS 
  select 
(select image from tblAuctionImage where auctionseq=goods.seq and seq = (select min(seq) from tblAuctionImage where auctionseq=goods.seq)) as imageName,
goods.seq, goods.title, status.status, bid.biddingPrice,
(select biddingPrice from tblBid where auctionstatusseq=2 and auctionseq=goods.seq) as bigPrice,
bid.memberseq
from tblAuctionGoods goods
inner join tblBid bid on goods.seq = bid.auctionseq 
inner join tblAuctionStatus status on status.seq = bid.auctionstatusseq
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View VWGOODSLOG
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "AUCTION"."VWGOODSLOG" ("SEQ", "AUCTIONSEQ", "BIGCATEGORYSEQ", "REGDATE") AS 
  select agl.seq,agl.auctionseq,gsc.bigcategoryseq,agl.regdate from tblauctiongoods ag inner join tblauctiongoodslog agl on ag.seq = agl.auctionseq 
inner join tblgoodssmallcategory gsc on ag.smallcategoryseq = gsc.seq
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View VWPURCHASEHISTORY
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "AUCTION"."VWPURCHASEHISTORY" ("IMAGENAME", "SEQ", "PAYDATE", "GOODNAME", "BIDDINGPRICE", "ESSTATUS", "RPSTATUS", "RFSTATUS", "MEMBERSEQ", "ISPAYED", "SHIPNUM") AS 
  select 
(select image from tblAuctionImage where auctionseq=goods.seq and seq = (select min(seq) from tblAuctionImage where auctionseq=goods.seq)) as imageName,
goods.seq, bid.payDate,goods.goodname,bid.biddingPrice, escrow.status as esStatus, report.status as rpStatus, refund.status as rfStatus,
bid.memberseq,bid.isPayed, ship.shipnum
from tblAuctionGoods goods
inner join tblEscrow escrow on goods.seq = escrow.auctionseq
inner join tblBid bid on goods.seq = bid.auctionseq
left outer join tblReport report on goods.seq = report.auctionseq
left outer join tblRefund refund on goods.seq = refund.auctionseq
left outer join tblShipping ship on ship.auctionseq = goods.seq
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View VWREFUNDHISTORY
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "AUCTION"."VWREFUNDHISTORY" ("SEQ", "SELLERSEQ", "GOODNAME", "DETAIL", "REGDATE", "EMAIL", "NAME") AS 
  select rf.seq,goods.memberseq as sellerseq, goods.goodname,rf.detail,rf.regdate ,member.email, member.name  from tblRefund rf 
inner join tblAuctionGoods goods on rf.auctionseq = goods.seq
inner join tblMember member on member.seq = rf.memberseq
;

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Procedure PROCINSERTAUCTIONGOOD
--------------------------------------------------------
set define off;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "AUCTION"."PROCINSERTAUCTIONGOOD" (
    pmemberseq number,
    psmallcategoryseq number, 
    ptitle varchar2,
    pgoodname varchar2,
    pdetail varchar2,
    pbrand varchar2,
    pstartprice number,
    pdeadline varchar2,
    pinstantprice number,
    pestimatedPrice number,
    paskingPrice number,
    pmainImg varchar2,
    psubImg1 varchar2,
    psubImg2 varchar2,
    psubImg3 varchar2
)
is 
    vauctionseq tblAuctionGoods.seq%type;
begin
    insert into tblAuctionGoods values(auctiongoods_seq.nextval,pmemberseq,psmallcategoryseq,ptitle,pgoodname,pdetail,pbrand,pstartprice,sysdate,pdeadline,pinstantprice,pestimatedPrice,paskingPrice,null,pstartprice);
    select max(seq) into vauctionseq from tblAuctionGoods;

    insert into tblAuctionImage values(AUCTIONIMAGE_SEQ.nextval,vauctionseq,pmainImg,1);
    insert into tblAuctionImage values(AUCTIONIMAGE_SEQ.nextval,vauctionseq,psubImg1,0);
    insert into tblAuctionImage values(AUCTIONIMAGE_SEQ.nextval,vauctionseq,psubImg2,0);
    insert into tblAuctionImage values(AUCTIONIMAGE_SEQ.nextval,vauctionseq,psubImg3,0);

commit;
exception
    when others then 
       rollback; 
end;

/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Procedure PROCINSERTAUCTIONGOODS
--------------------------------------------------------
set define off;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "AUCTION"."PROCINSERTAUCTIONGOODS" (
    pmemberseq number,
    psmallcategoryseq number, 
    ptitle varchar2,
    pgoodname varchar2,
    pdetail varchar2,
    pbrand varchar2,
    pstartprice number,
    pdeadline varchar2,
    pinstantprice number,
    pestimatedPrice number,
    paskingPrice number,
    pmainImg varchar2,
    psubImg1 varchar2,
    psubImg2 varchar2,
    psubImg3 varchar2
)
is 
    vauctionseq tblAuctionGoods.seq%type;
begin
    insert into tblAuctionGoods values(auctiongoods_seq.nextval,pmemberseq,psmallcategoryseq,ptitle,pgoodname,pdetail,pbrand,pstartprice,sysdate,pdeadline,pinstantprice,pestimatedPrice,paskingPrice,null,pstartprice);
    select max(seq) into vauctionseq from tblAuctionGoods;

    insert into tblAuctionImage values(AUCTIONIMAGE_SEQ.nextval,vauctionseq,pmainImg,1);
    insert into tblAuctionImage values(AUCTIONIMAGE_SEQ.nextval,vauctionseq,psubImg1,0);
    insert into tblAuctionImage values(AUCTIONIMAGE_SEQ.nextval,vauctionseq,psubImg2,0);
    insert into tblAuctionImage values(AUCTIONIMAGE_SEQ.nextval,vauctionseq,psubImg3,0);

commit;
exception
    when others then 
       rollback; 
end;

/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Procedure PROCINSERTBID
--------------------------------------------------------
set define off;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "AUCTION"."PROCINSERTBID" (
    pmemberseq varchar2,
    pauctionseq varchar2
)
is
    vmybiddingprice tblBid.biddingPrice%type;
begin
    select nowprice+askingprice into vmybiddingprice from tblAuctionGoods where seq = pauctionseq; 
    update tblAuctionGoods set nowPrice = vmybiddingprice where seq = pauctionseq;
    update tblMemberDetail set bonus = bonus + (vmybiddingprice/100) where memberseq = pmemberseq;
    insert into tblbid values(bid_seq.nextval,pauctionseq,pmemberseq,3,sysdate,vmybiddingprice,0,null);

    commit;
exception
    when others then 
       rollback; 
end;

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Procedure PROCWINNINGBID
--------------------------------------------------------
set define off;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "AUCTION"."PROCWINNINGBID" (
    pmemberseq in number,
    presult out sys_refcursor
)
is
begin
    open presult for
select * from(select ag.goodname, ts.status, b.biddingprice, 
(select max(tblBid.biddingprice) from tblBid where tblBid.auctionseq = b.auctionseq) as finalbiddingprice
    from tblBid b inner join tblAuctiongoods ag on b.auctionseq = ag.seq 
        inner join tblauctionstatus ts on b.auctionstatusseq = ts.seq
            where b.memberseq = pmemberseq) where biddingprice = (select max(biddingprice) from (select ag.goodname, ts.status, b.biddingprice, 
(select max(tblBid.biddingprice) from tblBid where tblBid.auctionseq = b.auctionseq) as finalbiddingprice
    from tblBid b inner join tblAuctiongoods ag on b.auctionseq = ag.seq 
        inner join tblauctionstatus ts on b.auctionstatusseq = ts.seq
            where b.memberseq = pmemberseq));
end;

--  DDL for Procedure PROC_MYBATIS_ADD
--------------------------------------------------------
set define off;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "AUCTION"."PROC_MYBATIS_ADD" (
    pName in varchar2,
    pAge in number
)
is
begin
    insert into tblMyBatis(seq,name,age) values(mybatis_seq.nextval,pName,pAge);
end;

select name from tblMyBatis where age = (select max(age) from tblMyBatis);

create or replace procedure proc_mybatis_get(
    pName out varchar2
)
is
begin
    select name into pName from tblMyBatis where age = (select max(age) from tblMyBatis) and seq = 7;
end;

 select name from tblMyBatis where age = (select max(age) from tblMyBatis) and seq =7;

create or replace procedure proc_mybatis_list(
    presult out sys_refcursor
)
is
begin
    open presult for
        select seq,name,age from tblMyBatis;
end;

select * from employees;
select distinct job_id from employees;
select last_name||' '||first_name,email,phone_number,job_id from employees where job_id='IT_PROG';
select last_name||' '||first_name as name ,email,phone_number as phone,job_id as job from employees;
select last_name||' '||first_name as name ,email,phone_number as phone,job_id as job from employees where first_name like '%ta%';

select * from employees;
select first_name as name, salary from employees;


select * from tblAuctionGoods ag inner join tblBid b on ag.seq = b.auctionseq where ag.seq=20;
